 Know what is the difference between Cash economy and Cashless economy: Cash transaction 1
 kisi bhi kharidari athwa bikwaali kaa sabase purana tarika cash tranjaction he
 The 18-million-crore currency demonetization process in the country's economy was before it began
 vahiin lagbhag 84 lakh karod rupye se adhik karency blike iconomi main maujuud hone kaa sarkari anumaan he
 2
 cash kaa istemaal kar tranjaction ko aasaani se karne ke liye badi se badi dinomination (500, 1000, 2000 rupye kii karency) zyada madadgaar sabit hoti he
 The biggest advantage of transacting through cash is that the said transaction can be done by hiding it from the bank or the government and as per the law, the tax payable on any transaction can also be avoided
 3
 Cash transaction is a very easy way
 yahaan kisi bhi kharidari ke badale sirf karency kii jarurat padati he
 Cash transactions are considered easy because the transaction is considered complete only on exchange of currency
 is madhyam main kharidaar ke paas sirf karency or bechney vaale ke paas sirf utpaada kaa rahanaa aavashyak he
 Cashless transaction 1
 cashles tranjaction digitaliseshan ke daur main teji se lokapriy hota madhyam he
 To buy or sell through this medium, both buyer and seller need to take support of the bank
 is madhyam main aapke bank ke saath-saath rigerv bank or sarkaar ke tex vibhaag kii bhi ahm bhoomika rahati he
 2
 cashles tranjaction ke liye plastic mani athwa credit or debit kaa sahaara liya jaataa he
 This card is given on opening an account with a bank
 iske alaava, bank kaa check or draft cashles tranjaction kii shrenee main aata he
 Digital wallets, mobile banking, NEFT and RTGS are also increasingly popular methods of cashless transactions
 3
 Cashless transactions are not as easy as cash
 lekin suraksha ke lihaaj se yah cash lene-dene se kaaphi behatar he
 This medium keeps every major transaction in the eyes of the bank and the tax department of the government
 vahiin chote se chote tranjaction kaa bhi puraa byora maujuud rahata he
 Cashless vs Cash1
 beete paanch saal ke dauraan desh main mobile banking main 1000 guna ijapha dekhne ko mila he
 2
 enift ke madhyas se cashles transfar main beete paanch varshon ke dauraan 20 guna ijapha hua he
 3
 bankig main artijies or check pement beete paanch saal ke dauraan mahaj do guna hua he
 4
 beete paanch saal ke dauraan check pement or net banking main giravat darj hui he
 5
 paanch saal pehle tak banking vyavastha main teen-chauthai pement check ke madhyam se kiya jaataa tha
 Now, keeping in mind these features and difficulties of cash transactions and cashless transactions, it is the effort of the government and the Reserve Bank to move the country from cash to cashless economy
 haalanki, iske liye behad jaruri he ki desh main bankig ko adhik popular kiya jaae
 Priority should be given not only to bring more and more population of the country under the ambit of banking but also to enable them to buy and sell through banking

 Tea is made in the house of all of us
 kisi ke ghar main do baar to kisi ke ghar main har ghante ke hisaab se
 After making tea, used tea leaves are dumped in the garbage in the homes of most of us
 lekin kya aap jaanate hai is chipatti ko aap kai tareeke se dobaaraa istemaal kar sakate hai
 As such, used tea leaves can be reused in many ways
 lekin iske liye bahut jaruri he ki aapako iske istemaal kaa sahi tarika pataa ho
 After making tea, clean the remaining tea leaves in the sieve thoroughly
 taaki usamen maujuud mithaas dur ho jaae
 The remaining tea leaves can be used in these tasks: 1
 chipatti main anti-oxident paae jate hai
 In this case, it is beneficial to apply tea paste on the injury or any wound
 ubili hui chipatti ko acchhee tarah dho len
 Applying it on the injury will heal the wound quickly
 iske alaava aap chahen to chipatti ko dhokar dobaaraa ubaal len
 Washing the wound with this water will also be beneficial
 2
 Chaipatti water is an excellent conditioner
 chipatti ko dhokar dobaaraa ubaal len
 Wash hair with this water
 isse baalachamakadaraur soft ho jaaenge
 3
 chipatti ko dobaaraa dhokar sukha len
 This tea leaf can be used while making kabuli gram
 isse chane kii rangath nikhar jaaegi
 4
 is chipatti ko dobaaraa ubaal len
 Cleaning the furniture by filling this water in a spray bottle
 issefurniture chamak uthenge
 5
 bachi hui chipatti ko acchhee tarah saaf kar len
 This tea leaf can also be used as a fertilizer
 austrailia kii prasiddh La trobe university ne apni sthapana kii 50veen varshganth par bharat se apane shiksha sambandhon ko majboot banane kaa prastaav rakhaa he
 In which it has announced the introduction of a new scholarship scheme for students with new universities in India
 laa trob uniwarsity ke professor jon dever or anya faikalti ne tay kiya he ki uniwarsity kii 50veen saalagirah par bharat ke 3 uniwarsity ke saath scolership yojana ko lekar partnership kii ghoshnaa kii

 pradhanmantri manmohan singh somvaar ko paanch din kii japan or thailand yatra par ravaanaa ho gaye
 The yatra focuses on giving new meaning to the 'look East' policy and hopes to contribute to peace, prosperity and stability in the Asia Pacific
 manmohan ne apane pehle padaav tokyo ke liye udaan bhari
 He described Japan as "an important regional and global partner for India"
 manmohan ne ravaanaa hone se purv apane bayaan main kaha ki vah raajnneetik, suraksha or urja kshetron main japan ke saath bharat ke sambandh majboot karne par baat karenge
 He said, 'my visit to Japan and Thailand will strengthen our' Look East Policy 'and it will get new meaning
 ’ teen divasiy japan yatra ke dauraan manmohan raksha sambandhon ko pragadh karne tathaa asainya parmaanu qaraar sahyog ke liye dwipaksheeya samjhaute ko aage badhaane par vimarsh karenge
 The Prime Minister will hold detailed discussions with host Prime Minister Shinzo Abe on various issues on Wednesday
 is dauraan raksha, aarthik, urja tathaa anya kshetron main sahyog badhaane par vishesh dhyaan diya jayega
 The Prime Minister said, 'the harmony of our interests is increasing and i see this relationship as an essential element of our vision for sustainable peace and prosperity in Asia
 ’singh ne japani pradhanmantri ebe ko apana bahut acha mitra bataaya or kaha ki donon deshon ke bich lagaataar shikhar baithkon se bharat-japan ranneetik evam vaishvik saajheedaari ko mili gati ko vah, ebe ke saath milakar or majbootee denge
 Regarding the civil nuclear cooperation agreement, Singh told Japanese reporters that there are problems in Japan and elections are due for the Upper House later this year
 unhone kaha ‘lekin mujhe ummid he ki ham asainya parmaanu urja sahyog main pragati kar sakate hai
 "I will try to use this journey to strengthen our strategic and global partnership, including trying to reach an agreement in terms of civil nuclear energy cooperation," Singh said

 akasar aisa tark diya jaataa he ki vibhinn subjects ko thodaa-thodaa jaanane se behatar he ki ek subject ko gaharaai se samajha ja saken

 antar bas itnaa he ki isamen aise vailu adishan kii pahchaan kii jaati he jo vibhinn vishyon ko ekasaath jodakar hasil kiya ja saktaa he

 However, the concept of Liberal Education has been a part of our heritage

 Today, with international boards such as the International Baccalaureate and IGCSE becoming popular, Liberal Education is returning again and colleges are also transforming themselves to promote multi-disciplinary studies
 shiksha ke is nae style se badhata parichay bharat main libral ajukeshan or libral arts collejon kii maujuudagi ko majboot banane kii disha main pehla kadam he

 In many countries April 1 is celebrated as Fool's Day
 yah aise din ke rup main janaa jaataa he, jab log aapas main vyavaharik majaak or moorkhtapurna harakatein karte hai
 There are different trends about Fool's Day in every country and people celebrate this day in different ways
 aise main jaanate hai ki aakhir is din kaa itihaas kya he or aakhir isaki shuruyaat kahaan or kab se kii gai
 
 
 There are many stories about April Fool
 itihaas par najar daali jaae to 1 april ke din kai phani ghatnaayen hui, jiske chalate is din ko april phool-de ke taur par manaaya jane laga
 April Fools' Day (fool's Day) is said to have started in France in 1582, when Pope Charles 9 replaced the old calendar with a new Roman calendar
 bataaya jaataa he ki is dauraan kuch log puraani taarikh par hi nayaa saal manaate rahe or unhen hi april fools kaha gaya
 However, many other stories about Fool's Day are also prevalent
 kai reports main daawa kiya jaataa he ki isaki shuruyaat 1392 bhi bataai jaati he, lekin iske koi pukhta pramaan nahin he
 At the same time, many reports said that in the year 1508, a French poet referred to a Poisson d'avril (april Fool)
 vahiin 1539 main flemish kavi 'de dene' ne ek amir aadmi ke bare main likhaa, jisane 1 april ko apane naukaron ko moorkhtapurna kaaryon ke liye bheja tha
 Many other similar stories are also prevalent
 har desh kii alag kahaneprail phool kii kahaniyon kii tarah ise manaane ke tareeke bhi kaaphi alag alag hai
 In France, Italy, Belgium, paper fish are made and pasted and mocked

 It is celebrated on 1 May in Denmark and is called Maj-kat
 vahiin spanish bolne vaale deshon main 28 disambar ko april phool manaaya jaataa he, jise de of holi inocents kaha jaataa he
